Note:  Mostly works, but USB dongle or the tablet module may go to sleep when inactive.  Re-establishing a connection could require a unplugging and reconnecting both.  Pen is a slightly jittery, like using two mice at once.  Driver can be misleading if it successfully sees the dongle that's not actually communicating with a tablet.  Tablet's wireless module appears to draw power exclusively from onboard battery, which may be long dead by now.
